Ensure workspace directory exists os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True) # Initialize search engine searcher = DDGS(timeout=20) print('TARGET PUBLICATION DETAILS:') print('‚Ä¢ Publisher: Center for U.S.-Mexican Studies') print('‚Ä¢ Year: 1992') print('‚Ä¢ Topic: Nineteenth-century Mexico') print('‚Ä¢ Chapter: Monterrey regional growth through war, trade, capitalism (1850-1910)') print('‚Ä¢ Goal: Identify editor and book title') print() # Simple, focused search queries search_queries = [ 'Center for U.S.-Mexican Studies 1992 Mexico publication', 'UC San Diego Mexican Studies 1992 book editor', 'Monterrey Mexico 1850-1910 capitalism war trade regional growth', 'Mexico regions comparative history development 1992', 'Center U.S.-Mexican Studies 1992 nineteenth-century Mexico editor' ] # Initialize simple results storage all_results = [] search_summary = { 'queries_executed': [], 'total_results_found': 0, 'relevant_findings': [], 'potential_books': [] } print('EXECUTING BASIC SEARCH STRATEGY') print('=' * 50) # Execute searches with basic error handling for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f'\n[SEARCH {i}/{len(search_queries)}] {query}') print('-' * 60) try: # Simple search execution results = searcher.text( query, max_results=6, backend=["duckduckgo", "bing"], safesearch="off", region="en-us" ) search_summary['queries_executed'].append(query) if results and len(results) > 0: print(f'Found {len(results)} results') for j, result in enumerate(results, 1): # Safely extract result data title = str(result.get('title', 'No title')) body = str(result.get('body', 'No description')) href = str(result.get('href', 'No URL')) print(f'\nResult {j}:') print(f'Title: {title}') print(f'Description: {body[:200]}...' if len(body) > 200 else f'Description: {body}') print(f'URL: {href}') # Simple relevance analysis text_content = (title + ' ' + body).lower() # Check for key terms key_indicators = { '1992': False, 'center': False, 'mexican studies': False, 'monterrey': False, 'mexico': False, 'editor': False, 'book': False, '1850': False, '1910': False, 'capitalism': False } # Simple term matching for term in key_indicators: if term in text_content: key_indicators[term] = True # Count matches matches = sum(key_indicators.values()) matched_terms = [term for term, found in key_indicators.items() if found] # Store result result_data = { 'query': query, 'title': title, 'body': body, 'url': href, 'matches': matches, 'matched_terms': matched_terms } all_results.append(result_data) search_summary['total_results_found'] += 1 # Categorize relevance if matches >= 4: print(f'üéØ HIGH RELEVANCE ({matches} matches): {", ".join(matched_terms)}') search_summary['relevant_findings'].append(result_data) # Check if this could be our target book if ('1992' in text_content and ('center' in text_content or 'mexican studies' in text_content) and ('book' in text_content or 'editor' in text_content)): print(' üìö POTENTIAL TARGET BOOK!') search_summary['potential_books'].append(result_data) elif matches >= 2: print(f'üìã Moderate relevance ({matches} matches): {", ".join(matched_terms)}') elif matches >= 1: print(f'üìù Low relevance ({matches} matches): {", ".join(matched_terms)}') print('-' * 40) else: print('No results found for this query') except Exception as e: print(f'Error during search: {str(e)}') print('Continuing with next query...') # Simple rate limiting time.sleep(3) print('=' * 60) # Analysis and summary print('\n' + '=' * 80) print('SEARCH RESULTS ANALYSIS') print('=' * 80) print(f'\nüìä SEARCH STATISTICS:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Queries executed: {len(search_summary["queries_executed"])}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total results found: {search_summary["total_results_found"]}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Relevant findings: {len(search_summary["relevant_findings"])}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Potential target books: {len(search_summary["potential_books"])}') # Display relevant findings if search_summary['relevant_findings']: print(f'\nüîç RELEVANT FINDINGS ({len(search_summary["relevant_findings"])}):') print('-' * 50) for i, finding in enumerate(search_summary['relevant_findings'], 1): print(f'\n{i}. {finding["title"]}') print(f' Matches: {finding["matches"]} - {', '.join(finding["matched_terms"])}') print(f' Description: {finding["body"][:150]}...') print(f' URL: {finding["url"]}') # Display potential books if search_summary['potential_books']: print(f'\nüìö POTENTIAL TARGET BOOKS ({len(search_summary["potential_books"])}):') print('-' * 50) for i, book in enumerate(search_summary['potential_books'], 1): print(f'\nüéØ BOOK CANDIDATE {i}:') print(f' Title: {book["title"]}') print(f' Matches: {book["matches"]} - {', '.join(book["matched_terms"])}') print(f' Description: {book["body"][:200]}...') print(f' URL: {book["url"]}') # Check for editor information text_to_check = (book['title'] + ' ' + book['body']).lower() if 'editor' in text_to_check or 'edited by' in text_to_check: print(' ‚úÖ CONTAINS EDITOR INFORMATION!') else: print('\n‚ùå No potential target books identified') print('\nRECOMMENDATIONS:') print('1. Try more specific searches with author names') print('2. Search for "Mexico\'s Regions" as this appears in results') print('3. Look for UC San Diego faculty publications from 1992') print('4. Contact Center for U.S.-Mexican Studies directly') # Save results to workspace results_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'simple_mexican_studies_search_results.json') with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump({ 'search_summary': search_summary, 'all_results': all_results, 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') }, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüíæ SEARCH RESULTS SAVED TO: {results_file}') # Look for specific patterns in high-relevance results print('\n' + '=' * 60) print('DETAILED ANALYSIS OF HIGH-RELEVANCE RESULTS') print('=' * 60) if search_summary['relevant_findings']: for finding in search_summary['relevant_findings']: text_content = (finding['title'] + ' ' + finding['body']).lower() # Look for specific book titles or editors if 'mexico\'s regions' in text_content: print(f'\nüìñ FOUND "MEXICO\'S REGIONS" REFERENCE:') print(f' Title: {finding["title"]}') print(f' Description: {finding["body"][:300]}...') print(f' URL: {finding["url"]}') # Look for 1992 publications if '1992' in text_content and ('center' in text_content or 'mexican studies' in text_content): print(f'\nüìÖ 1992 CENTER PUBLICATION REFERENCE:') print(f' Title: {finding["title"]}') print(f' Description: {finding["body"][:300]}...') print(f' URL: {finding["url"]}') # Look for Monterrey economic history if 'monterrey' in text_content and any(term in text_content for term in ['1850', '1910', 'capitalism', 'trade']): print(f'\nüè≠ MONTERREY ECONOMIC HISTORY REFERENCE:') print(f' Title: {finding["title"]}') print(f' Description: {finding["body"][:300]}...') print(f' URL: {finding["url"]}') print('\nüéØ NEXT STEPS:') if search_summary['potential_books']: print('1. ‚úÖ Investigate potential book candidates for complete details') print('2. ‚úÖ Follow up on editor information in findings') print('3. ‚úÖ Verify publication details and chapter contents') else: print('1. üîÑ Search specifically for "Mexico\'s Regions Comparative History Development"') print('2. üîÑ Look for Mario Cerutti as potential author/editor (appeared in results)') print('3. üîÑ Search UC San Diego institutional repositories') print('4. üîÑ Try WorldCat or library catalog searches') print('\n=== SIMPLE SEARCH EXECUTION COMPLETE ===')

### Development Step 4: Locate 1851 Atheistic Naturalism Phrenology Mesmerism Book and 2009 Reissuing Publisher

**Description**: Conduct a comprehensive web search to identify a co-authored book from 1851 that advocated for atheistic naturalism, systematically explored phrenology and mesmerism, was controversial for these topics, and was reissued by a publisher in 2009. Search using keywords including '1851 book atheistic naturalism phrenology mesmerism co-authored', '1851 controversial book phrenology mesmerism reissued 2009', 'atheistic naturalism 1851 publication', and 'phrenology mesmerism 1851 authors'. Focus on identifying both the original 1851 publication details and the specific publisher who reissued it in 2009.

**Use Cases**:
- University research library digitization team using the multi-engine search script to locate and verify obscure 1851 scientific texts for digital archive inclusion and confirm 2009 reissue details.
- Historical society librarian employing automated Google Scholar, Bing, JSTOR, and archive.org queries to compile a complete bibliography of co-authored controversial phrenology and mesmerism treatises for a museum exhibition.
- Digital humanities scholar mapping the spread of atheistic naturalism by systematically harvesting primary sources and modern reprint information from multiple search engines for network analysis.
- Rare bookseller validating a potential 1851 first edition‚Äôs provenance by cross-referencing academic databases and general web searches to confirm authorship, publication history, and a 2009 specialty press reissue.
- PhD candidate in history of science leveraging the Python multi-method search to uncover mid-19th century philosophical works on phrenology and mesmerism across library catalogs and online archives for dissertation research.
- Independent publisher‚Äôs research team discovering forgotten public domain texts for annotated reissues by scanning academic sites and search engines to identify obscure co-authored volumes and track modern rights holders.
- Data journalist investigating the revival of fringe-science publications by extracting publication metadata and reissue patterns from search logs to illustrate how 19th-century controversial works reappear in contemporary niche markets.

```
import os
import requests
import json
import time

from bs4 import BeautifulSoup

print('Implementing multi-pronged approach with different search engines and methods\n')

# Ensure workspace directory exists
os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True)

# Initialize comprehensive results storage

'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
'objective': 'Find 1851 co-authored book on atheistic naturalism with phrenology/mesmerism, reissued 2009',
'search_methods': [],
'all_findings': [],
'book_candidates': [],
'analysis_summary': {}
}

]

'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,*/*;q=0.8',
'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.9',
'Accept-Encoding': 'gzip, deflate, br',
'Connection': 'keep-alive'
}

for i, query in enumerate(scholar_queries, 1):
print(f'\nGoogle Scholar Search {i}: {query}')
try:
scholar_url = f'https://scholar.google.com/scholar?q={quote_plus(query)}'
print(f'URL: {scholar_url}')

response = requests.get(scholar_url, headers=headers, timeout=20)
print(f'Status: {response.status_code}')

if response.status_code == 200:
# Save raw HTML
filename = f'google_scholar_search_{i}.html'
filepath = os.path.join('workspace', filename)
with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write(response.text)
print(f'Saved: {filepath}')

# Quick parse for academic results
soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser')

# Look for result titles in Google Scholar
result_titles = soup.find_all(['h3', 'a'], class_=lambda x: x and 'gs_rt' in str(x))
if not result_titles:
result_titles = soup.find_all('h3')

print(f'Found {len(result_titles)} potential results')

for j, title_elem in enumerate(result_titles[:5], 1):

if len(title_text) > 10:
print(f' {j}. {title_text[:100]}...')

# Check for key terms
text_lower = title_text.lower()
relevance_indicators = []
if '1851' in text_lower: relevance_indicators.append('1851')
if 'phrenology' in text_lower: relevance_indicators.append('phrenology')
if 'mesmerism' in text_lower: relevance_indicators.append('mesmerism')
if 'naturalism' in text_lower: relevance_indicators.append('naturalism')

if relevance_indicators:
print(f' ‚≠ê Relevant terms: {', '.join(relevance_indicators)}')
search_results['all_findings'].append({
'source': 'Google Scholar',
'query': query,
'title': title_text,
'relevance_terms': relevance_indicators,
'method': 'scholar_direct'
})

search_results['search_methods'].append(f'Google Scholar: {query} - Status {response.status_code}')
else:
print(f'Failed with status {response.status_code}')

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error: {str(e)}')

time.sleep(3) # Rate limiting

if len(link_text) > 15 and href:

relevance_score = 0
matched_terms = []

key_terms = {'1851': 3, 'phrenology': 2, 'mesmerism': 2, 'naturalism': 2, 'atheistic': 2, 'book': 1}

for term, weight in key_terms.items():
if term in text_lower:
relevance_score += weight
matched_terms.append(term)

if relevance_score >= 3:
relevant_results.append({
'text': link_text[:150],
'href': href,
'score': relevance_score,
'terms': matched_terms
})

'relevance_score': result['score'],

'method': 'bing_direct'
})

search_results['search_methods'].append(f'Bing: {query} - Status {response.status_code}')
else:

})

else:
print(f'Failed with status {response.status_code}')

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error: {str(e)}')

if search_results['all_findings']:
print('\nüîç ALL FINDINGS ANALYSIS:')

# Group by source

for finding in search_results['all_findings']:

if source not in by_source:
by_source[source] = []
by_source[source].append(finding)

for source, findings in by_source.items():

for i, finding in enumerate(findings, 1):
title = finding.get('title', finding.get('snippet', 'No title'))[:100]

year_indicators = ['1851']
topic_indicators = ['phrenology', 'mesmerism', 'naturalism', 'atheistic']

for finding in search_results['all_findings']:
text_content = (finding.get('title', '') + ' ' + finding.get('snippet', '')).lower()

has_book = any(indicator in text_content for indicator in book_indicators)
has_year = any(indicator in text_content for indicator in year_indicators)
has_topic = any(indicator in text_content for indicator in topic_indicators)

if has_book and has_year and has_topic:
search_results['book_candidates'].append(finding)

print(f'\nüìö POTENTIAL BOOK CANDIDATES: {len(search_results["book_candidates"])}')
for i, candidate in enumerate(search_results['book_candidates'], 1):
print(f'\n{i}. Source: {candidate["source"]}')
print(f' Title/Snippet: {candidate.get("title", candidate.get("snippet", "No content"))[:150]}...')

# Save comprehensive results

### Development Step 1: Find Nedoshivina 2010 Publication Describing Kuznetzov‚Äôs Vietnamese Specimens, Including Methods and Repository Info

**Description**: Search for Nedoshivina's 2010 scientific paper that includes descriptions of Vietnamese specimens by Kuznetzov. Focus on finding the complete publication with methods/materials sections or specimen repository information. Use these search approaches: (1) Academic databases like Google Scholar, PubMed, or ResearchGate using keywords 'Nedoshivina 2010 Vietnamese specimens Kuznetzov', (2) Taxonomic databases that might reference specimen deposits, (3) Journal archives that published the paper in 2010. Look specifically for sections mentioning specimen deposition, museum collections, or institutional repositories where the Vietnamese materials were stored.

**Use Cases**:
- Entomology researcher retrieving Nedoshivina‚Äôs 2010 paper to verify Vietnamese veneer moth specimen depositories before describing a new related species
- Museum curator cross-referencing taxonomic literature to confirm the institutional repository and accession numbers of Kuznetzov‚Äôs Vietnam collection for database curation
- Graduate student compiling methods and material details from primary sources to support a molecular phylogeny of Southeast Asian Tortricidae
- Biodiversity informatics specialist automating DOI and PDF link extraction for taxonomic publications to integrate specimen metadata into an online species portal

- Academic librarian indexing obscure entomological articles in digital archives, using SerpAPI to locate full-text PDFs and DOIs for 2010 publications

```
import os
import re
import requests

# Search for Nedoshivina's 2010 scientific paper that includes descriptions of Vietnamese specimens by Kuznetzov
query = '"Nedoshivina" 2010 Vietnamese specimens Kuznetzov'
max_results = 15
type = "search"

# Get SerpAPI key from environment variables
api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY")

if api_key is None:
print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.")
else:
print(f"Searching for: {query}")
print(f"API key available: {api_key[:10]}...")

# Prepare API request parameters
params = {
"q": query,
"api_key": api_key,
"engine": "google",
"google_domain": "google.com",
"safe": "off",
"num": max_results,
"type": type,
}

print(f"Making request to SerpAPI with params: {params}")

# Make API request to SerpAPI
response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params)

print(f"Response status code: {response.status_code}")

if response.status_code == 200:
results = response.json()

# Check if we got organic results
if not results.get("organic_results"):
print(f"No results found for '{query}'. Response keys: {list(results.keys())}")
if 'error' in results:
print(f"API Error: {results['error']}")

# Try a broader search
print("\nTrying a broader search with just 'Nedoshivina 2010'...")
broad_query = "Nedoshivina 2010"
params["q"] = broad_query

response2 = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params)
if response2.status_code == 200:
results2 = response2.json()
if results2.get("organic_results"):
results = results2
query = broad_query
print(f"Broader search successful with {len(results['organic_results'])} results")

if results.get("organic_results"):
print(f"\nFound {len(results['organic_results'])} results for '{query}':")
print("="*80)

# Look for academic paper links (PDF, DOI, journal sites)
academic_links = []
relevant_results = []

for i, result in enumerate(results["organic_results"]):
title = result.get('title', 'No title')
link = result.get('link', 'No link')
snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet')

print(f"\nResult {i+1}:")
print(f"Title: {title}")
print(f"Link: {link}")
print(f"Snippet: {snippet}")
print("-" * 60)

# Check for academic/scientific indicators
academic_indicators = [
'doi.org', 'pubmed', 'researchgate', 'scholar.google',
'.pdf', 'journal', 'publication', 'research',
'specimens', 'taxonomy', 'species', 'museum',
'repository', 'collection', 'vietnam'
]

is_academic = any(indicator in (title + link + snippet).lower() for indicator in academic_indicators)

if is_academic:
academic_links.append(link)
relevant_results.append(result)
print(f"*** POTENTIALLY RELEVANT ACADEMIC SOURCE ***")

# Check specifically for Vietnamese/specimen content
vietnamese_indicators = ['vietnam', 'specimen', 'kuznetzov', 'collection', 'museum', 'repository']
has_vietnamese_content = any(indicator in (title + link + snippet).lower() for indicator in vietnamese_indicators)

if has_vietnamese_content:
print(f"*** CONTAINS VIETNAMESE/SPECIMEN CONTENT ***")

print(f"\nTotal potentially academic links found: {len(academic_links)}")
for i, link in enumerate(academic_links[:5]): # Show first 5
print(f"Academic link {i+1}: {link}")

# Save search results to workspace
import json
search_data = {
'query_used': query,
'total_results': len(results['organic_results']),
'academic_links_found': len(academic_links),
'search_results': results,
'relevant_results': relevant_results
}

with open('workspace/nedoshivina_2010_search_results.json', 'w') as f:
json.dump(search_data, f, indent=2)
print(f"\nSearch results saved to workspace/nedoshivina_2010_search_results.json")

# Try more specific searches if initial search wasn't very successful
if len(academic_links) < 3:
print("\n" + "="*80)
print("CONDUCTING ADDITIONAL TARGETED SEARCHES")
print("="*80)

additional_queries = [
'"Nedoshivina" Vietnamese specimens taxonomy',
'Kuznetzov Vietnamese specimens 2010',
'Nedoshivina 2010 filetype:pdf',
'"Nedoshivina" museum collection Vietnam'
]

all_additional_results = []

for additional_query in additional_queries:
print(f"\nSearching: {additional_query}")
params["q"] = additional_query
params["num"] = 10 # Fewer results for additional searches

add_response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params)
if add_response.status_code == 200:
add_results = add_response.json()
if add_results.get("organic_results"):
print(f"Found {len(add_results['organic_results'])} additional results")
all_additional_results.extend(add_results['organic_results'])

# Show top results for this search
for j, result in enumerate(add_results['organic_results'][:3]):
title = result.get('title', 'No title')
link = result.get('link', 'No link')
print(f" {j+1}. {title[:100]}...")
print(f" {link}")
else:
print("No results for this additional query")
else:
print(f"Error in additional search: {add_response.status_code}")

# Save all additional search results
if all_additional_results:
additional_data = {
'additional_queries': additional_queries,
'total_additional_results': len(all_additional_results),
'additional_search_results': all_additional_results
}

with open('workspace/nedoshivina_additional_searches.json', 'w') as f:
json.dump(additional_data, f, indent=2)
print(f"\nAdditional search results saved to workspace/nedoshivina_additional_searches.json")
print(f"Total additional results found: {len(all_additional_results)}")

else:
print(f"Error: API request failed with status {response.status_code}: {response.text}")
```

### Development Step 5: Identify 1851 Atheistic Naturalism Book on Phrenology/Mesmerism and Its 2009 Reissue Publisher

**Description**: Conduct a comprehensive web search to identify a co-authored book from 1851 that advocated for atheistic naturalism, systematically explored phrenology and mesmerism, was controversial for these topics, and was reissued by a publisher in 2009. Search using keywords including '1851 book atheistic naturalism phrenology mesmerism co-authored', '1851 controversial book phrenology mesmerism reissued 2009', 'atheistic naturalism 1851 publication', and 'phrenology mesmerism 1851 authors'. Focus on identifying both the original 1851 publication details and the specific publisher who reissued it in 2009.

**Use Cases**:
- Academic historian automating the identification of obscure 19th-century texts and their modern reissue details for a journal article on atheistic naturalism controversies
- Library metadata specialist using targeted web and scholarly search scripts to update collection records with publication dates, co-authors, and reprint publisher information
- Digital humanities project integrating automated web scraping and match-scoring to curate a dataset of phrenology and mesmerism publications for network and discourse analysis
- Publishing house acquisitions team conducting due diligence on public domain works by detecting original 1851 publication details and 2009 reissue rights before green-lighting a new edition
- Intellectual property attorney verifying authorship, publication history, and modern publisher claims for 19th-century texts in a litigation involving contested reprint rights
- Graduate student building a reproducible search pipeline to gather evidence on historical debates in naturalism, phrenology, and mesmerism for a dissertation timeline and annotated bibliography
- Cultural heritage institution employing automated Google Scholar analysis to tag and contextualize controversial topics in its digital archive of 19th-century manuscripts
- Open-access repository manager using a customized search-and-analyze workflow to prioritize the digitization of historically significant works with detailed bibliographic provenance

```
import os
import json
from collections import Counter

search_data = json.load(f)

print(f'File keys: {list(search_data.keys())}')
print(f'Timestamp: {search_data.get("timestamp", "N/A")}')
print(f'Total findings: {len(search_data.get("all_findings", []))}')
print(f'Search methods: {len(search_data.get("search_methods", []))}')

if search_data.get('all_findings'):
print(f'\nFirst finding structure: {list(search_data["all_findings"][0].keys())}')
print(f'Sample finding: {search_data["all_findings"][0]}')
else:
print('‚ùå No previous search results file found')
# Initialize empty structure
search_data = {
'timestamp': 'N/A',
'all_findings': [],
'search_methods': [],
'book_candidates': []
}

print('\n' + '='*80)
print('DETAILED ANALYSIS OF GOOGLE SCHOLAR FINDINGS')
print('='*80)

# Analyze the Google Scholar findings in detail
scholar_findings = [f for f in search_data.get('all_findings', []) if f.get('source') == 'Google Scholar']

print(f'Google Scholar findings to analyze: {len(scholar_findings)}')

if scholar_findings:
print('\nüìö DETAILED ANALYSIS OF EACH FINDING:')
print('-' * 60)

potential_1851_books = []
related_works = []

for i, finding in enumerate(scholar_findings, 1):
title = finding.get('title', 'No title')
terms = finding.get('relevance_terms', [])
query = finding.get('query', 'Unknown query')

print(f'\n{i}. TITLE: {title}')
print(f' QUERY: {query}')
print(f' RELEVANT TERMS: {", ".join(terms)}')

# Analyze for 1851 connections
title_lower = title.lower()

# Check for year indicators
year_indicators = ['1851', '1850', '1852', 'mid-19th', '19th century']
has_year = any(indicator in title_lower for indicator in year_indicators)

# Check for book indicators
book_indicators = ['book', 'letters', 'treatise', 'work', 'volume']
has_book = any(indicator in title_lower for indicator in book_indicators)

# Check for naturalism/atheism indicators
naturalism_indicators = ['naturalism', 'atheistic', 'atheism', 'scientific', 'natural']
has_naturalism = any(indicator in title_lower for indicator in naturalism_indicators)

# Check for co-authorship indicators
coauthor_indicators = ['letters', 'correspondence', 'dialogue']
has_coauthor_hint = any(indicator in title_lower for indicator in coauthor_indicators)

print(f' ANALYSIS:')
print(f' - Year connection: {has_year} ({[y for y in year_indicators if y in title_lower]})')
print(f' - Book format: {has_book} ({[b for b in book_indicators if b in title_lower]})')
print(f' - Naturalism theme: {has_naturalism} ({[n for n in naturalism_indicators if n in title_lower]})')
print(f' - Co-author hints: {has_coauthor_hint} ({[c for c in coauthor_indicators if c in title_lower]})')

# Score potential match
match_score = 0
if has_year: match_score += 3
if has_book: match_score += 2
if has_naturalism: match_score += 2
if has_coauthor_hint: match_score += 1
if 'phrenology' in terms: match_score += 2
if 'mesmerism' in terms: match_score += 2

print(f' - MATCH SCORE: {match_score}/12')

if match_score >= 6:
print(' ‚≠ê HIGH POTENTIAL MATCH')
potential_1851_books.append({
'title': title,
'score': match_score,
'terms': terms,
'analysis': {
'has_year': has_year,
'has_book': has_book,
'has_naturalism': has_naturalism,
'has_coauthor_hint': has_coauthor_hint
}
})
elif match_score >= 3:
print(' üìñ RELATED WORK')
related_works.append({
'title': title,
'score': match_score,
'terms': terms
})

print(f'\n\nüéØ POTENTIAL 1851 BOOK MATCHES: {len(potential_1851_books)}')
print('='*60)

if potential_1851_books:
# Sort by score
potential_1851_books.sort(key=lambda x: x['score'], reverse=True)

for i, book in enumerate(potential_1851_books, 1):
print(f'\n{i}. {book["title"]}')
print(f' Score: {book["score"]}/12')
print(f' Terms: {", ".join(book["terms"])}')
print(f' Year connection: {book["analysis"]["has_year"]}')
print(f' Book format: {book["analysis"]["has_book"]}')
print(f' Naturalism theme: {book["analysis"]["has_naturalism"]}')
print(f' Co-author hints: {book["analysis"]["has_coauthor_hint"]}')
else:
print('No high-scoring matches found in current results')

print(f'\nüìö RELATED WORKS: {len(related_works)}')
print('='*40)

if related_works:
related_works.sort(key=lambda x: x['score'], reverse=True)
for i, work in enumerate(related_works[:5], 1): # Show top 5
print(f'{i}. {work["title"]} (Score: {work["score"]})')

else:
print('No Google Scholar findings to analyze')

# Now conduct more targeted searches based on the most promising finding
print('\n' + '='*80)

import requests

for i, query in enumerate(targeted_queries, 1):

try:
# Try Google search
google_url = f'https://www.google.com/search?q={quote_plus(query)}'
print(f'URL: {google_url}')

response = requests.get(google_url, headers=headers, timeout=20)
print(f'Status: {response.status_code}')

if response.status_code == 200:
# Save HTML
filename = f'targeted_search_{i}_{query[:30].replace(" ", "_").replace("\'", "")}.html'
filepath = os.path.join('workspace', filename)

with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write(response.text)

print(f'Saved: {filepath}')

# Quick parse for results
soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser')

# Look for result snippets and titles
result_elements = soup.find_all(['h3', 'div', 'span'], string=lambda text: text and any(term in text.lower() for term in ['1851', 'letters', 'martineau', 'atkinson', 'phrenology', 'mesmerism', '2009']))

relevant_snippets = []
for elem in result_elements:
text = elem.get_text().strip()
if len(text) > 20 and len(text) < 300:
text_lower = text.lower()
relevance_terms = []

key_terms = ['1851', 'letters', 'martineau', 'atkinson', 'phrenology', 'mesmerism', 'naturalism', 'atheistic', '2009', 'reissue']

for term in key_terms:
if term in text_lower:
relevance_terms.append(term)

if len(relevance_terms) >= 2:
relevant_snippets.append({
'text': text,
'terms': relevance_terms,
'query': query
})

print(f'Found {len(relevant_snippets)} relevant snippets')

for j, snippet in enumerate(relevant_snippets[:3], 1):
print(f' {j}. {snippet["text"][:100]}...')
print(f' Terms: {", ".join(snippet["terms"])}')

targeted_results.append(snippet)

else:
print(f'Failed with status {response.status_code}')

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error: {str(e)}')

time.sleep(3) # Rate limiting

print('\n' + '='*80)
print('COMPREHENSIVE FINDINGS SUMMARY')
print('='*80)

print(f'üìä SEARCH STATISTICS:')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Previous Google Scholar findings: {len(scholar_findings)}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ High-potential 1851 book matches: {len(potential_1851_books) if "potential_1851_books" in locals() else 0}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Related works identified: {len(related_works) if "related_works" in locals() else 0}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Targeted search results: {len(targeted_results)}')

# Compile all evidence

import os import requests import json import time from urllib.parse import quote_plus from bs4 import BeautifulSoup print('=== SEARCHING FOR ERIC VAN YOUNG MEXICAN RURAL HISTORY ARTICLES ===') print('Objective: Find when Eric Van Young published articles on Mexican rural history') print('Focus: Rural Mexico, agricultural history, peasant studies, countryside dynamics\n') # Ensure workspace directory exists os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True) # Initialize search results storage search_results = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'objective': 'Find Eric Van Young articles on Mexican rural history and publication years', 'search_queries': [], 'all_findings': [], 'academic_articles': [], 'publication_years': [], 'search_methods': [] } print('TARGET CRITERIA:') print('‚Ä¢ Author: Eric Van Young') print('‚Ä¢ Topic: Mexican rural history') print('‚Ä¢ Subtopics: Agricultural history, peasant studies, countryside social dynamics') print('‚Ä¢ Goal: Identify specific publication years for rural Mexico articles\n') # Method 1: Try SerpAPI Google Scholar search first print('=== METHOD 1: GOOGLE SCHOLAR VIA SERPAPI ===') print('=' * 60) # Get SerpAPI key from environment variables api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key: print(f'SerpAPI key available: {api_key[:10]}...') # Define targeted search queries scholar_queries = [ 'Eric Van Young Mexican rural history', 'Eric Van Young peasant Mexico', 'Eric Van Young agricultural history Mexico', 'Eric Van Young countryside Mexico', '"Eric Van Young" rural Mexico articles' ] for i, query in enumerate(scholar_queries, 1): print(f'\nGoogle Scholar Search {i}: {query}') try: # Prepare API request parameters for Google Scholar params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google_scholar", "num": 20, # Get more results for comprehensive search "start": 0 } print(f'Making SerpAPI request...') response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params) print(f'Response status: {response.status_code}') if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() # Check for organic results in Google Scholar if results.get("organic_results"): print(f'Found {len(results["organic_results"])} Google Scholar results') for j, result in enumerate(results["organic_results"], 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') authors = result.get('authors', 'No authors') year = result.get('year', 'No year') snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet') link = result.get('link', 'No link') print(f'\n Result {j}:') print(f' Title: {title}') print(f' Authors: {authors}') print(f' Year: {year}') print(f' Snippet: {snippet[:150]}...' if len(snippet) > 150 else f' Snippet: {snippet}') print(f' Link: {link}') # Check relevance to rural Mexico topics combined_text = f'{title} {authors} {snippet}'.lower() rural_indicators = ['rural', 'peasant', 'agricultural', 'countryside', 'village', 'hacienda', 'agrarian'] mexico_indicators = ['mexico', 'mexican', 'nueva espa√±a', 'new spain'] has_rural = any(indicator in combined_text for indicator in rural_indicators) has_mexico = any(indicator in combined_text for indicator in mexico_indicators) has_van_young = 'van young' in combined_text or 'eric' in combined_text if has_rural and has_mexico and has_van_young: print(f' ‚≠ê HIGHLY RELEVANT: Rural Mexico + Van Young') article_data = { 'title': title, 'authors': authors, 'year': year, 'snippet': snippet, 'link': link, 'query': query, 'source': 'Google Scholar (SerpAPI)', 'relevance_score': 3, 'rural_indicators': [ind for ind in rural_indicators if ind in combined_text], 'mexico_indicators': [ind for ind in mexico_indicators if ind in combined_text] } search_results['academic_articles'].append(article_data) if year and year != 'No year': search_results['publication_years'].append(year) elif (has_rural or has_mexico) and has_van_young: print(f' üìñ POTENTIALLY RELEVANT') article_data = { 'title': title, 'authors': authors, 'year': year, 'snippet': snippet, 'link': link, 'query': query, 'source': 'Google Scholar (SerpAPI)', 'relevance_score': 2 if has_rural else 1 } search_results['all_findings'].append(article_data) search_results['search_methods'].append(f'Google Scholar SerpAPI: {query} - {len(results["organic_results"])} results') else: print('No organic results found') if 'error' in results: print(f'API Error: {results["error"]}') else: print(f'SerpAPI request failed: {response.status_code} - {response.text[:200]}') except Exception as e: print(f'Error in SerpAPI search: {str(e)}') time.sleep(2) # Rate limiting search_results['search_queries'].extend(scholar_queries) else: print('‚ùå No SerpAPI key available, skipping Google Scholar search') # Method 2: Direct web search using requests print('\n=== METHOD 2: DIRECT WEB SEARCH ===') print('=' * 50) headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36', 'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,*/*;q=0.8', 'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.9' } # Try Google search directly web_queries = [ '"Eric Van Young" Mexican rural history articles', '"Eric Van Young" peasant Mexico publication', 'Eric Van Young agricultural history Mexico academic', '"Eric Van Young" countryside Mexico research' ] for i, query in enumerate(web_queries, 1): print(f'\nWeb Search {i}: {query}') try: google_url = f'https://www.google.com/search?q={quote_plus(query)}' print(f'URL: {google_url}') response = requests.get(google_url, headers=headers, timeout=20) print(f'Status: {response.status_code}') if response.status_code == 200: # Save HTML for analysis filename = f'eric_van_young_search_{i}.html' filepath = os.path.join('workspace', filename) with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(response.text) print(f'Saved: {filepath}') # Parse for academic results soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') # Look for result links and snippets result_links = soup.find_all('a', href=True) academic_results = [] for link in result_links: link_text = link.get_text().strip() href = link.get('href') if len(link_text) > 20 and href: text_lower = link_text.lower() # Check for academic indicators academic_indicators = ['jstor', 'academia.edu', 'researchgate', 'doi.org', 'journal', 'university', 'press'] van_young_indicators = ['van young', 'eric'] rural_indicators = ['rural', 'peasant', 'agricultural', 'countryside', 'agrarian'] mexico_indicators = ['mexico', 'mexican'] has_academic = any(indicator in (text_lower + href.lower()) for indicator in academic_indicators) has_van_young = any(indicator in text_lower for indicator in van_young_indicators) has_rural = any(indicator in text_lower for indicator in rural_indicators) has_mexico = any(indicator in text_lower for indicator in mexico_indicators) if has_academic and has_van_young and (has_rural or has_mexico): academic_results.append({ 'text': link_text[:200], 'href': href, 'has_rural': has_rural, 'has_mexico': has_mexico, 'query': query }) print(f'Found {len(academic_results)} potentially academic results') for j, result in enumerate(academic_results[:5], 1): print(f' {j}. {result["text"][:100]}...') print(f' Rural: {result["has_rural"]}, Mexico: {result["has_mexico"]}') print(f' Link: {result["href"][:80]}...') search_results['all_findings'].append({ 'title': result['text'], 'link': result['href'], 'query': query, 'source': 'Google Web Search', 'has_rural_content': result['has_rural'], 'has_mexico_content': result['has_mexico'] }) search_results['search_methods'].append(f'Google Web: {query} - Status {response.status_code}') else: print(f'Failed with status {response.status_code}') except Exception as e: print(f'Error: {str(e)}') time.sleep(3) # Rate limiting search_results['search_queries'].extend(web_queries) # Method 3: Try academic-specific searches print('\n=== METHOD 3: ACADEMIC DATABASE SEARCHES ===') print('=' * 55) # Search specific academic sites academic_sites = [ 'site:jstor.org', 'site:academia.edu', 'site:researchgate.net', 'site:muse.jhu.edu' ] base_query = '"Eric Van Young" Mexican rural' for i, site in enumerate(academic_sites, 1): query = f'{site} {base_query}' print(f'\nAcademic Search {i}: {query}') try: google_url = f'https://www.google.com/search?q={quote_plus(query)}' print(f'URL: {google_url}') response = requests.get(google_url, headers=headers, timeout=20) print(f'Status: {response.status_code}') if response.status_code == 200: filename = f'academic_search_{i}_{site.replace("site:", "").replace(".", "_")}.html' filepath = os.path.join('workspace', filename) with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(response.text) print(f'Saved: {filepath}') # Quick parse for results soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') # Look for Google result titles and snippets result_titles = soup.find_all(['h3', 'div'], class_=lambda x: x and ('BNeawe' in str(x) or 'LC20lb' in str(x))) relevant_titles = [] for title_elem in result_titles: title_text = title_elem.get_text().strip() if len(title_text) > 10: text_lower = title_text.lower() if 'van young' in text_lower and ('rural' in text_lower or 'mexico' in text_lower): relevant_titles.append(title_text) print(f'Found {len(relevant_titles)} relevant titles') for j, title in enumerate(relevant_titles[:3], 1): print(f' {j}. {title[:120]}...') search_results['all_findings'].append({ 'title': title, 'query': query, 'source': f'Academic - {site}', 'method': 'academic_site_search' }) search_results['search_methods'].append(f'Academic {site}: Status {response.status_code}') else: print(f'Failed with status {response.status_code}') except Exception as e: print(f'Error: {str(e)}') time.sleep(4) # Longer delay for Google # Analyze all findings print('\n' + '='*80) print('COMPREHENSIVE ANALYSIS OF ERIC VAN YOUNG SEARCH RESULTS') print('='*80) total_findings = len(search_results['all_findings']) academic_articles = len(search_results['academic_articles']) publication_years = list(set(search_results['publication_years'])) # Remove duplicates print(f'üìä SEARCH STATISTICS:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total findings: {total_findings}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Academic articles (high relevance): {academic_articles}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Publication years identified: {len(publication_years)}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Search methods attempted: {len(search_results["search_methods"])}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Queries executed: {len(search_results["search_queries"])}') if academic_articles > 0: print(f'\nüéØ HIGH-RELEVANCE ACADEMIC ARTICLES:') print('-' * 50) # Sort by year if available sorted_articles = sorted(search_results['academic_articles'], key=lambda x: x.get('year', '0000'), reverse=True) for i, article in enumerate(sorted_articles, 1): print(f'\n{i}. TITLE: {article["title"]}') print(f' AUTHORS: {article["authors"]}') print(f' YEAR: {article["year"]}') print(f' RURAL TERMS: {article.get("rural_indicators", [])}') print(f' MEXICO TERMS: {article.get("mexico_indicators", [])}') print(f' SNIPPET: {article["snippet"][:200]}...') print(f' SOURCE: {article["source"]}') print(f' LINK: {article["link"]}') if publication_years: print(f'\nüìÖ PUBLICATION YEARS IDENTIFIED:') print('-' * 40) sorted_years = sorted(publication_years) for year in sorted_years: articles_in_year = [a for a in search_results['academic_articles'] if a.get('year') == year] print(f' ‚Ä¢ {year}: {len(articles_in_year)} article(s)') for article in articles_in_year: print(f' - {article["title"][:80]}...') else: print('\n‚ùå No specific publication years identified') print('This could mean:') print('1. Articles found but years not clearly extracted') print('2. Need more targeted searches') print('3. Information may be in full-text articles rather than abstracts') # Save comprehensive results results_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'eric_van_young_rural_mexico_search.json') with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(search_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüíæ COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH RESULTS SAVED TO: {results_file}') # Summary and recommendations print(f'\nüéØ SEARCH SUMMARY:') if academic_articles > 0: print('‚úÖ SUCCESS: Found Eric Van Young articles on Mexican rural history') if publication_years: earliest_year = min(publication_years) latest_year = max(publication_years) print(f'‚úÖ Publication timeframe: {earliest_year} to {latest_year}') else: print('‚ö†Ô∏è PARTIAL: Articles found but specific years need verification') else: print('‚ö†Ô∏è LIMITED: Few high-relevance articles found in current search') print(f'\nüìã NEXT STEPS:') if academic_articles > 0: print('1. ‚úÖ Review identified articles for exact publication years') print('2. ‚úÖ Follow links to full articles for detailed verification') print('3. ‚úÖ Cross-reference with Eric Van Young\'s CV or bibliography') else: print('1. üîÑ Try searches with specific book titles by Eric Van Young') print('2. üîÑ Search university websites for his faculty profile') print('3. üîÑ Look for his complete bibliography or CV online') print('4. üìÅ Review all saved HTML files for additional context') print('5. üîç Consider searching for specific works like "The Other Rebellion"') print('\n=== ERIC VAN YOUNG MEXICAN RURAL HISTORY SEARCH COMPLETE ===')

import os import requests import json import time from urllib.parse import quote_plus from bs4 import BeautifulSoup print('=== SEARCHING FOR ERIC VAN YOUNG MEXICAN RURAL HISTORY ARTICLES ===') print('Objective: Find when Eric Van Young published articles on Mexican rural history') print('Focus: Rural Mexico, agricultural history, peasant studies, countryside dynamics\n') # Ensure workspace directory exists os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True) # Initialize search results storage search_results = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'objective': 'Find Eric Van Young articles on Mexican rural history and publication years', 'search_queries': [], 'all_findings': [], 'academic_articles': [], 'publication_years': [], 'search_methods': [] } print('TARGET CRITERIA:') print('‚Ä¢ Author: Eric Van Young') print('‚Ä¢ Topic: Mexican rural history') print('‚Ä¢ Subtopics: Agricultural history, peasant studies, countryside social dynamics') print('‚Ä¢ Goal: Identify specific publication years for rural Mexico articles\n') # Method 1: Try SerpAPI Google Scholar search first print('=== METHOD 1: GOOGLE SCHOLAR VIA SERPAPI ===') print('=' * 60) # Get SerpAPI key from environment variables api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key: print(f'SerpAPI key available: {api_key[:10]}...') # Define targeted search queries scholar_queries = [ 'Eric Van Young Mexican rural history', 'Eric Van Young peasant Mexico', 'Eric Van Young agricultural history Mexico', 'Eric Van Young countryside Mexico', '"Eric Van Young" rural Mexico articles' ] for i, query in enumerate(scholar_queries, 1): print(f'\nGoogle Scholar Search {i}: {query}') try: # Prepare API request parameters for Google Scholar params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google_scholar", "num": 20, # Get more results for comprehensive search "start": 0 } print(f'Making SerpAPI request...') response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params) print(f'Response status: {response.status_code}') if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() # Check for organic results in Google Scholar if results.get("organic_results"): print(f'Found {len(results["organic_results"])} Google Scholar results') for j, result in enumerate(results["organic_results"], 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') authors = result.get('authors', 'No authors') year = result.get('year', 'No year') snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet') link = result.get('link', 'No link') print(f'\n Result {j}:') print(f' Title: {title}') print(f' Authors: {authors}') print(f' Year: {year}') print(f' Snippet: {snippet[:150]}...' if len(snippet) > 150 else f' Snippet: {snippet}') print(f' Link: {link}') # Check relevance to rural Mexico topics combined_text = f'{title} {authors} {snippet}'.lower() rural_indicators = ['rural', 'peasant', 'agricultural', 'countryside', 'village', 'hacienda', 'agrarian'] mexico_indicators = ['mexico', 'mexican', 'nueva espa√±a', 'new spain'] has_rural = any(indicator in combined_text for indicator in rural_indicators) has_mexico = any(indicator in combined_text for indicator in mexico_indicators) has_van_young = 'van young' in combined_text or 'eric' in combined_text if has_rural and has_mexico and has_van_young: print(f' ‚≠ê HIGHLY RELEVANT: Rural Mexico + Van Young') article_data = { 'title': title, 'authors': authors, 'year': year, 'snippet': snippet, 'link': link, 'query': query, 'source': 'Google Scholar (SerpAPI)', 'relevance_score': 3, 'rural_indicators': [ind for ind in rural_indicators if ind in combined_text], 'mexico_indicators': [ind for ind in mexico_indicators if ind in combined_text] } search_results['academic_articles'].append(article_data) if year and year != 'No year': search_results['publication_years'].append(year) elif (has_rural or has_mexico) and has_van_young: print(f' üìñ POTENTIALLY RELEVANT') article_data = { 'title': title, 'authors': authors, 'year': year, 'snippet': snippet, 'link': link, 'query': query, 'source': 'Google Scholar (SerpAPI)', 'relevance_score': 2 if has_rural else 1 } search_results['all_findings'].append(article_data) search_results['search_methods'].append(f'Google Scholar SerpAPI: {query} - {len(results["organic_results"])} results') else: print('No organic results found') if 'error' in results: print(f'API Error: {results["error"]}') else: print(f'SerpAPI request failed: {response.status_code} - {response.text[:200]}') except Exception as e: print(f'Error in SerpAPI search: {str(e)}') time.sleep(2) # Rate limiting search_results['search_queries'].extend(scholar_queries) else: print('‚ùå No SerpAPI key available, skipping Google Scholar search') # Method 2: Direct web search using requests print('\n=== METHOD 2: DIRECT WEB SEARCH ===') print('=' * 50) headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36', 'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,*/*;q=0.8', 'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.9' } # Try Google search directly web_queries = [ '"Eric Van Young" Mexican rural history articles', '"Eric Van Young" peasant Mexico publication', 'Eric Van Young agricultural history Mexico academic', '"Eric Van Young" countryside Mexico research' ] for i, query in enumerate(web_queries, 1): print(f'\nWeb Search {i}: {query}') try: google_url = f'https://www.google.com/search?q={quote_plus(query)}' print(f'URL: {google_url}') response = requests.get(google_url, headers=headers, timeout=20) print(f'Status: {response.status_code}') if response.status_code == 200: # Save HTML for analysis filename = f'eric_van_young_search_{i}.html' filepath = os.path.join('workspace', filename) with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(response.text) print(f'Saved: {filepath}') # Parse for academic results soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') # Look for result links and snippets result_links = soup.find_all('a', href=True) academic_results = [] for link in result_links: link_text = link.get_text().strip() href = link.get('href') if len(link_text) > 20 and href: text_lower = link_text.lower() # Check for academic indicators academic_indicators = ['jstor', 'academia.edu', 'researchgate', 'doi.org', 'journal', 'university', 'press'] van_young_indicators = ['van young', 'eric'] rural_indicators = ['rural', 'peasant', 'agricultural', 'countryside', 'agrarian'] mexico_indicators = ['mexico', 'mexican'] has_academic = any(indicator in (text_lower + href.lower()) for indicator in academic_indicators) has_van_young = any(indicator in text_lower for indicator in van_young_indicators) has_rural = any(indicator in text_lower for indicator in rural_indicators) has_mexico = any(indicator in text_lower for indicator in mexico_indicators) if has_academic and has_van_young and (has_rural or has_mexico): academic_results.append({ 'text': link_text[:200], 'href': href, 'has_rural': has_rural, 'has_mexico': has_mexico, 'query': query }) print(f'Found {len(academic_results)} potentially academic results') for j, result in enumerate(academic_results[:5], 1): print(f' {j}. {result["text"][:100]}...') print(f' Rural: {result["has_rural"]}, Mexico: {result["has_mexico"]}') print(f' Link: {result["href"][:80]}...') search_results['all_findings'].append({ 'title': result['text'], 'link': result['href'], 'query': query, 'source': 'Google Web Search', 'has_rural_content': result['has_rural'], 'has_mexico_content': result['has_mexico'] }) search_results['search_methods'].append(f'Google Web: {query} - Status {response.status_code}') else: print(f'Failed with status {response.status_code}') except Exception as e: print(f'Error: {str(e)}') time.sleep(3) # Rate limiting search_results['search_queries'].extend(web_queries) # Method 3: Try academic-specific searches print('\n=== METHOD 3: ACADEMIC DATABASE SEARCHES ===') print('=' * 55) # Search specific academic sites academic_sites = [ 'site:jstor.org', 'site:academia.edu', 'site:researchgate.net', 'site:muse.jhu.edu' ] base_query = '"Eric Van Young" Mexican rural' for i, site in enumerate(academic_sites, 1): query = f'{site} {base_query}' print(f'\nAcademic Search {i}: {query}') try: google_url = f'https://www.google.com/search?q={quote_plus(query)}' print(f'URL: {google_url}') response = requests.get(google_url, headers=headers, timeout=20) print(f'Status: {response.status_code}') if response.status_code == 200: filename = f'academic_search_{i}_{site.replace("site:", "").replace(".", "_")}.html' filepath = os.path.join('workspace', filename) with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(response.text) print(f'Saved: {filepath}') # Quick parse for results soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') # Look for Google result titles and snippets result_titles = soup.find_all(['h3', 'div'], class_=lambda x: x and ('BNeawe' in str(x) or 'LC20lb' in str(x))) relevant_titles = [] for title_elem in result_titles: title_text = title_elem.get_text().strip() if len(title_text) > 10: text_lower = title_text.lower() if 'van young' in text_lower and ('rural' in text_lower or 'mexico' in text_lower): relevant_titles.append(title_text) print(f'Found {len(relevant_titles)} relevant titles') for j, title in enumerate(relevant_titles[:3], 1): print(f' {j}. {title[:120]}...') search_results['all_findings'].append({ 'title': title, 'query': query, 'source': f'Academic - {site}', 'method': 'academic_site_search' }) search_results['search_methods'].append(f'Academic {site}: Status {response.status_code}') else: print(f'Failed with status {response.status_code}') except Exception as e: print(f'Error: {str(e)}') time.sleep(4) # Longer delay for Google # Analyze all findings print('\n' + '='*80) print('COMPREHENSIVE ANALYSIS OF ERIC VAN YOUNG SEARCH RESULTS') print('='*80) total_findings = len(search_results['all_findings']) academic_articles = len(search_results['academic_articles']) publication_years = list(set(search_results['publication_years'])) # Remove duplicates print(f'üìä SEARCH STATISTICS:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total findings: {total_findings}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Academic articles (high relevance): {academic_articles}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Publication years identified: {len(publication_years)}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Search methods attempted: {len(search_results["search_methods"])}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Queries executed: {len(search_results["search_queries"])}') if academic_articles > 0: print(f'\nüéØ HIGH-RELEVANCE ACADEMIC ARTICLES:') print('-' * 50) # Sort by year if available sorted_articles = sorted(search_results['academic_articles'], key=lambda x: x.get('year', '0000'), reverse=True) for i, article in enumerate(sorted_articles, 1): print(f'\n{i}. TITLE: {article["title"]}') print(f' AUTHORS: {article["authors"]}') print(f' YEAR: {article["year"]}') print(f' RURAL TERMS: {article.get("rural_indicators", [])}') print(f' MEXICO TERMS: {article.get("mexico_indicators", [])}') print(f' SNIPPET: {article["snippet"][:200]}...') print(f' SOURCE: {article["source"]}') print(f' LINK: {article["link"]}') if publication_years: print(f'\nüìÖ PUBLICATION YEARS IDENTIFIED:') print('-' * 40) sorted_years = sorted(publication_years) for year in sorted_years: articles_in_year = [a for a in search_results['academic_articles'] if a.get('year') == year] print(f' ‚Ä¢ {year}: {len(articles_in_year)} article(s)') for article in articles_in_year: print(f' - {article["title"][:80]}...') else: print('\n‚ùå No specific publication years identified') print('This could mean:') print('1. Articles found but years not clearly extracted') print('2. Need more targeted searches') print('3. Information may be in full-text articles rather than abstracts') # Save comprehensive results results_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'eric_van_young_rural_mexico_search.json') with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(search_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüíæ COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH RESULTS SAVED TO: {results_file}') # Summary and recommendations print(f'\nüéØ SEARCH SUMMARY:') if academic_articles > 0: print('‚úÖ SUCCESS: Found Eric Van Young articles on Mexican rural history') if publication_years: earliest_year = min(publication_years) latest_year = max(publication_years) print(f'‚úÖ Publication timeframe: {earliest_year} to {latest_year}') else: print('‚ö†Ô∏è PARTIAL: Articles found but specific years need verification') else: print('‚ö†Ô∏è LIMITED: Few high-relevance articles found in current search') print(f'\nüìã NEXT STEPS:') if academic_articles > 0: print('1. ‚úÖ Review identified articles for exact publication years') print('2. ‚úÖ Follow links to full articles for detailed verification') print('3. ‚úÖ Cross-reference with Eric Van Young\'s CV or bibliography') else: print('1. üîÑ Try searches with specific book titles by Eric Van Young') print('2. üîÑ Search university websites for his faculty profile') print('3. üîÑ Look for his complete bibliography or CV online') print('4. üìÅ Review all saved HTML files for additional context') print('5. üîç Consider searching for specific works like "The Other Rebellion"') print('\n=== ERIC VAN YOUNG MEXICAN RURAL HISTORY SEARCH COMPLETE ===')

# Fix the NameError bug and properly analyze Eric Van Young search results import os import json import re from collections import Counter print('=== FIXING BUG AND ANALYZING ERIC VAN YOUNG SEARCH RESULTS ===') print('Previous execution failed due to NameError: combined_text not defined') print('Need to fix the bug and properly analyze the retrieved search data\n') # First, inspect the saved search results file structure results_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'eric_van_young_rural_mexico_search.json') if os.path.exists(results_file): print('üìÅ INSPECTING SAVED SEARCH RESULTS FILE:') print('-' * 50) with open(results_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: search_data = json.load(f) print(f'File keys: {list(search_data.keys())}') print(f'Timestamp: {search_data.get("timestamp", "N/A")}') print(f'Total findings: {len(search_data.get("all_findings", []))}') print(f'Academic articles: {len(search_data.get("academic_articles", []))}') print(f'Search methods: {len(search_data.get("search_methods", []))}') # Check if there are any search queries that returned results search_methods = search_data.get('search_methods', []) print(f'\nSearch methods executed: {len(search_methods)}') for method in search_methods: print(f' - {method}') else: print('‚ùå No previous search results file found') search_data = {'all_findings': [], 'academic_articles': [], 'search_methods': []} print('\n' + '='*80) print('RE-EXECUTING GOOGLE SCHOLAR ANALYSIS WITH BUG FIX') print('='*80) # Now let's re-run the Google Scholar search with the bug fixed import requests import time # Get SerpAPI key api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key: print(f'SerpAPI key available: {api_key[:10]}...') # Define targeted search queries for Eric Van Young scholar_queries = [ 'Eric Van Young Mexican rural history', 'Eric Van Young peasant Mexico', '"Eric Van Young" hacienda Mexico', '"Eric Van Young" colonial Mexico rural', 'Eric Van Young agrarian Mexico' ] # Initialize results storage fixed_results = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'objective': 'Find Eric Van Young articles on Mexican rural history with publication years', 'academic_articles': [], 'publication_years': [], 'all_findings': [], 'search_methods': [] } for i, query in enumerate(scholar_queries, 1): print(f'\nGoogle Scholar Search {i}: {query}') try: # Prepare API request parameters for Google Scholar params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google_scholar", "num": 20, "start": 0 } print(f'Making SerpAPI request...') response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params) print(f'Response status: {response.status_code}') if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() # Check for organic results in Google Scholar if results.get("organic_results"): print(f'Found {len(results["organic_results"])} Google Scholar results') for j, result in enumerate(results["organic_results"], 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') authors = result.get('authors', 'No authors') year = result.get('year', 'No year') snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet') link = result.get('link', 'No link') print(f'\n Result {j}:') print(f' Title: {title}') print(f' Authors: {authors}') print(f' Year: {year}') print(f' Snippet: {snippet[:150]}...' if len(snippet) > 150 else f' Snippet: {snippet}') print(f' Link: {link}') # FIX THE BUG: Define combined_text before using it combined_text = f'{title} {authors} {snippet}'.lower() # Check relevance to rural Mexico topics rural_indicators = ['rural', 'peasant', 'agricultural', 'countryside', 'village', 'hacienda', 'agrarian'] mexico_indicators = ['mexico', 'mexican', 'nueva espa√±a', 'new spain'] van_young_indicators = ['van young', 'eric'] has_rural = any(indicator in combined_text for indicator in rural_indicators) has_mexico = any(indicator in combined_text for indicator in mexico_indicators) has_van_young = any(indicator in combined_text for indicator in van_young_indicators) # Extract year information more carefully extracted_year = year if year == 'No year' or not year: # Try to extract year from title or snippet year_pattern = r'\b(19\d{2}|20\d{2})\b' year_match = re.search(year_pattern, combined_text) if year_match: extracted_year = year_match.group(1) print(f' Extracted year from text: {extracted_year}') if has_rural and has_mexico and has_van_young: print(f' ‚≠ê HIGHLY RELEVANT: Rural Mexico + Van Young') # Find specific rural and Mexico terms that matched matched_rural = [ind for ind in rural_indicators if ind in combined_text] matched_mexico = [ind for ind in mexico_indicators if ind in combined_text] article_data = { 'title': title, 'authors': authors, 'year': extracted_year, 'snippet': snippet, 'link': link, 'query': query, 'source': 'Google Scholar (SerpAPI)', 'relevance_score': 3, 'rural_indicators': matched_rural, 'mexico_indicators': matched_mexico, 'has_van_young': has_van_young } fixed_results['academic_articles'].append(article_data) if extracted_year and extracted_year != 'No year': fixed_results['publication_years'].append(extracted_year) print(f' üìÖ Publication year: {extracted_year}') elif (has_rural or has_mexico) and has_van_young: print(f' üìñ POTENTIALLY RELEVANT') article_data = { 'title': title, 'authors': authors, 'year': extracted_year, 'snippet': snippet, 'link': link, 'query': query, 'source': 'Google Scholar (SerpAPI)', 'relevance_score': 2 if has_rural else 1, 'has_rural': has_rural, 'has_mexico': has_mexico, 'has_van_young': has_van_young } fixed_results['all_findings'].append(article_data) if extracted_year and extracted_year != 'No year': fixed_results['publication_years'].append(extracted_year) fixed_results['search_methods'].append(f'Google Scholar SerpAPI: {query} - {len(results["organic_results"])} results') else: print('No organic results found') if 'error' in results: print(f'API Error: {results["error"]}') else: print(f'SerpAPI request failed: {response.status_code} - {response.text[:200]}') except Exception as e: print(f'Error in SerpAPI search: {str(e)}') time.sleep(2) # Rate limiting # Analysis of results print('\n' + '='*80) print('COMPREHENSIVE ANALYSIS OF FIXED SEARCH RESULTS') print('='*80) total_findings = len(fixed_results['all_findings']) academic_articles = len(fixed_results['academic_articles']) publication_years = list(set(fixed_results['publication_years'])) # Remove duplicates print(f'üìä CORRECTED SEARCH STATISTICS:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total findings: {total_findings}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Academic articles (high relevance): {academic_articles}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Publication years identified: {len(publication_years)}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Search methods completed: {len(fixed_results["search_methods"])}') if academic_articles > 0: print(f'\nüéØ HIGH-RELEVANCE ACADEMIC ARTICLES:') print('-' * 50) # Sort by year if available sorted_articles = sorted(fixed_results['academic_articles'], key=lambda x: x.get('year', '0000'), reverse=True) for i, article in enumerate(sorted_articles, 1): print(f'\n{i}. TITLE: {article["title"]}') print(f' AUTHORS: {article["authors"]}') print(f' YEAR: {article["year"]}') print(f' RURAL TERMS: {article.get("rural_indicators", [])}') print(f' MEXICO TERMS: {article.get("mexico_indicators", [])}') print(f' SNIPPET: {article["snippet"][:200]}...') print(f' SOURCE: {article["source"]}') print(f' LINK: {article["link"]}') if publication_years: print(f'\nüìÖ PUBLICATION YEARS IDENTIFIED:') print('-' * 40) sorted_years = sorted(publication_years) for year in sorted_years: articles_in_year = [a for a in fixed_results['academic_articles'] if a.get('year') == year] print(f' ‚Ä¢ {year}: {len(articles_in_year)} article(s)') for article in articles_in_year: print(f' - {article["title"][:80]}...') print(f'\nüéØ KEY FINDING: Eric Van Young published articles on Mexican rural history in:') for year in sorted_years: print(f' ‚≠ê {year}') else: print('\n‚ùå No specific publication years identified from current search') print('Need to examine the found articles more closely for year information') # Save corrected results corrected_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'eric_van_young_corrected_search.json') with open(corrected_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(fixed_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüíæ CORRECTED SEARCH RESULTS SAVED TO: {corrected_file}') # Final summary print(f'\nüéØ FINAL SUMMARY:') if academic_articles > 0 and publication_years: print('‚úÖ SUCCESS: Found Eric Van Young articles on Mexican rural history with publication years') earliest_year = min(publication_years) latest_year = max(publication_years) print(f'‚úÖ Publication timeframe: {earliest_year} to {latest_year}') print(f'‚úÖ Total relevant articles: {academic_articles}') # Highlight the most significant finding if publication_years: most_common_year = Counter(fixed_results['publication_years']).most_common(1)[0][0] print(f'‚úÖ Most active publication year: {most_common_year}') else: print('‚ö†Ô∏è PARTIAL: Search executed successfully but limited relevant results found') print(' This may indicate need for more specific search terms or different databases') else: print('‚ùå No SerpAPI key available - cannot execute Google Scholar search') print('Will analyze any existing saved HTML files instead') # Try to extract information from saved HTML files html_files = [f for f in os.listdir('workspace') if f.endswith('.html') and 'eric_van_young' in f] if html_files: print(f'\nFound {len(html_files)} HTML files to analyze:') for html_file in html_files: print(f' - {html_file}') # Analyze the first few HTML files for any year information from bs4 import BeautifulSoup extracted_years = [] for html_file in html_files[:3]: # Analyze first 3 files filepath = os.path.join('workspace', html_file) print(f'\nAnalyzing: {html_file}') try: with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: html_content = f.read() soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser') text_content = soup.get_text().lower() # Look for years in the text year_pattern = r'\b(19\d{2}|20\d{2})\b' years_found = re.findall(year_pattern, text_content) # Filter for reasonable publication years reasonable_years = [y for y in years_found if 1950 <= int(y) <= 2023] if reasonable_years: print(f' Found potential years: {set(reasonable_years)}') extracted_years.extend(reasonable_years) except Exception as e: print(f' Error analyzing {html_file}: {str(e)}') if extracted_years: unique_years = sorted(set(extracted_years)) print(f'\nüìÖ YEARS EXTRACTED FROM HTML FILES: {unique_years}') else: print('\n‚ùå No clear publication years found in HTML files') else: print('\n‚ùå No HTML files found to analyze') print('\n=== BUG FIX AND ANALYSIS COMPLETE ===')

Get SerpAPI key api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key: print(f'SerpAPI key available: {api_key[:10]}...') # Initialize results storage final_results = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'objective': 'Find Eric Van Young articles on Mexican rural history with publication years', 'academic_articles': [], 'publication_years': [], 'all_findings': [], 'search_methods': [], 'key_publications': [] } # Define targeted search queries scholar_queries = [ 'Eric Van Young Mexican rural history', 'Eric Van Young peasant Mexico', '"Eric Van Young" hacienda Mexico', '"Eric Van Young" colonial Mexico rural', 'Eric Van Young agrarian Mexico' ] for i, query in enumerate(scholar_queries, 1): print(f'\nGoogle Scholar Search {i}: {query}') try: # Define combined_text FIRST before any other operations combined_text = f'{title} {authors} {snippet}'.lower() print(f'\n Result {j}:') print(f' Title: {title}') print(f' Authors: {authors}') print(f' Year: {year}') print(f' Snippet: {snippet[:150]}...' if len(snippet) > 150 else f' Snippet: {snippet}') print(f' Link: {link}') # Now safely use combined_text for analysis rural_indicators = ['rural', 'peasant', 'agricultural', 'countryside', 'village', 'hacienda', 'agrarian'] mexico_indicators = ['mexico', 'mexican', 'nueva espa√±a', 'new spain'] van_young_indicators = ['van young', 'eric'] has_rural = any(indicator in combined_text for indicator in rural_indicators) has_mexico = any(indicator in combined_text for indicator in mexico_indicators) has_van_young = any(indicator in combined_text for indicator in van_young_indicators) # Look for year immediately after the phrase phrase_pattern = rf'{phrase}\s*(19\d{{2}}|20\d{{2}})' phrase_match = re.search(phrase_pattern, combined_text) if phrase_match: publication_year = phrase_match.group(1) print(f' üìÖ Found publication phrase: "{phrase} {publication_year}"') extracted_year = publication_year break # For debugging } final_results['academic_articles'].append(article_data) if extracted_year and extracted_year != 'No year': final_results['publication_years'].append(extracted_year) print(f' üìÖ Publication year recorded: {extracted_year}') elif (has_rural or has_mexico) and has_van_young: print(f' üìñ POTENTIALLY RELEVANT') article_data = { 'title': title, 'authors': authors, 'year': extracted_year, 'snippet': snippet, 'link': link, 'query': query, 'source': 'Google Scholar (SerpAPI)', 'relevance_score': 2 if has_rural else 1, 'has_rural': has_rural, 'has_mexico': has_mexico, 'has_van_young': has_van_young } final_results['all_findings'].append(article_data) if extracted_year and extracted_year != 'No year': final_results['publication_years'].append(extracted_year) # WORK: {pub["work_title"]}') print(f' YEAR: {pub["year"]}') print(f' EVIDENCE: {pub["evidence"]}') print(f' MENTIONED IN: {pub["mentioned_in"]}') if publication_years: print(f'\nüìÖ PUBLICATION YEARS IDENTIFIED:') print('-' * 40) sorted_years = sorted(publication_years) for year in sorted_years: articles_in_year = [a for a in final_results['academic_articles'] if a.get('year') == year] key_pubs_in_year = [k for k in final_results['key_publications'] if k.get('year') == year] total_in_year = len(articles_in_year) + len(key_pubs_in_year) print(f' ‚Ä¢ {year}: {total_in_year} publication(s)') for article in articles_in_year: print(f' - Get SerpAPI key api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key: print(f'SerpAPI key available: {api_key[:10]}...') # Initialize results storage final_results = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'objective': 'Find Eric Van Young articles on Mexican rural history with publication years', 'academic_articles': [], 'publication_years': [], 'all_findings': [], 'search_methods': [], 'key_publications': [] } # Define combined_text FIRST before any other operations combined_text = f'{title} {authors} {snippet}'.lower() print(f'\n Result {j}:') print(f' Title: {title}') print(f' Authors: {authors}') print(f' Year: {year}') print(f' Snippet: {snippet[:150]}...' if len(snippet) > 150 else f' Snippet: {snippet}') print(f' Link: {link}') # Now safely use combined_text for analysis rural_indicators = ['rural', 'peasant', 'agricultural', 'countryside', 'village', 'hacienda', 'agrarian'] mexico_indicators = ['mexico', 'mexican', 'nueva espa√±a', 'new spain'] van_young_indicators = ['van young', 'eric'] has_rural = any(indicator in combined_text for indicator in rural_indicators) has_mexico = any(indicator in combined_text for indicator in mexico_indicators) has_van_young = any(indicator in combined_text for indicator in van_young_indicators) # Extract year information more carefully extracted_year = year if year == 'No year' or not year: # Try to extract year from title or snippet using regex year_pattern = r'\b(19\d{2}|20\d{2})\b' year_matches = re.findall(year_pattern, combined_text) if year_matches: # Filter for reasonable publication years reasonable_years = [y for y in year_matches if 1950 <= int(y) <= 2023] if reasonable_years: extracted_year = reasonable_years[0] # Take the first reasonable year print(f' Extracted year from text: {extracted_year}') # Check for specific mentions of publication years in snippet publication_phrases = ['appeared in', 'published in', 'first appeared in', 'when it first appeared in'] for phrase in publication_phrases: if phrase in combined_text: # Look for year immediately after the phrase phrase_pattern = rf'{phrase}\s*(19\d{{2}}|20\d{{2}})' phrase_match = re.search(phrase_pattern, combined_text) if phrase_match: publication_year = phrase_match.group(1) print(f' üìÖ Found publication phrase: "{phrase} {publication_year}"') extracted_year = publication_year break #
